< Review>
Always so fun! It's HOT so bring your own water bottles. There is parking a great veggie stand and fruit stand if you don't feel like picking fruit yourself. Excellent local honey too!!! However,  not a good place for pets because there is no shade if they stay in the car, and too hot and sticky for them in the fields....Bring shoes that you don't mind getting a little dirty. Enjoy!<//Review>

< Review>
They usually have whatever produce is in season all summer.  Nice setting. Large parking. They had a coffee drive through although I can't guarantee that it is still there. If it is, it's really good coffee. They have a nice picnic area if you bring a picnic or want to eat some of your fruit before you leave. They have u-pick and already picked produce. Nice people run the place and the produce is very good. I recommend.<//Review>

Steak

Beer-Battered Fish

Rice

Taco condiments
5 different salsas

<user>104500642485315142392</user><pics>None</pics>< text>
A solid fast casual Mexican restaurant. All the food I have tried in this place is fine. I would say it's probably the best mexican food in that price range in the immediate area. It's convenient but it is also not my first choice for Mexican.

The reason for the 3 stars vs 5 is that it just isn't great and at least twice I have felt unwelcomed, sometimes the tables are dirty for a long time and same goes for the salsa bar. With that said, I used to go there almost every Saturday for breakfast.

Most recently, the owner made some comments to the manager about a customer being there "too long" on his laptop (they used to have wifi for customers). I was that customer and it felt really awkward. Unwelcome moment #1.

A couple weeks later, the wifi was removed and it seems that the original manager was let go.

When I came back, the first thing the new cashier told me wasn't "welcome," or "good morning," it was literally:

"just so you know, there is no more wifi"

Seems that maybe they were expecting me since I had never met that cashier before. Why would that be the first thing you tell a customer? Unwelcome moment #2.

It felt like "aha! No wifi for you!" Like the soup nazi from Seinfeld.

That whole experience left a very sour taste in my mouth, and demonstrated poor customer service.< /text>

My husband and I flew into San Diego from Seattle for our anniversary and had heard about Bombay from a friend that lived there. They said the food was amazing and they had belly dancers with snakes and fire....immediately we were in. We tried the chicken tandoori, aloo gobi, tikka masala and the rice....AMAZING! This was the best Indian food I have ever had...hands down! The service was fantastic as well. Ellie was our server and made sure that our dinner was perfect. <time>1408742617411</time>< text>
I was taking a stroll around Hillcrest for lunch and came across this nice Indian restaurant.  What immediately drew my attention was the $9.95 lunch special, which was posted outside of the entrance.  When I came in, I was immediately greeted and shown to my table.  The waiters were very courteous and offered different types of naan bread - I recall a spicy, garlic, and plain naan bread.  After choosing my bread, I made way to the buffet.  One section had the salads, the middle section had the different types of soups and curry (lentil soup, banana curry, eggplant, chicken tiki masala, vegetables to name a few), and then the desserts.

Everything tasted pretty good and for $9.95, definitely worth the trip.<//text>

I ate at Bombay last night and can't believe they are trying to defend themselves with this nonsense (comment from 9/19/10). <username>Duncan Leung<//username><Time>1472582277735< /Time>< Rate>
2<//Rate>
<resp>None< /resp>< Review>
Summary:
Get your recalls fixed at a dealership only because they're free. Besides that, I highly recommend an independent garage to do your other maintenance services.

I did more research and finally went with Corner 3 Garage for my other servicing/maintenance needs. The customer service there is honest, and they walk you through why different parts of your car need servicing, and what is really necessary to purchase/replace.

I received a 2004 Tundra with over 240,000 miles from my uncle so I wanted to make sure that it got a good servicing and that any recalls would be addressed, so I brought it to the Tustin Toyota dealership at 6:45am.

After diagnostics my service rep quoted:
$730 - Timing belt change
$249 - Front brakes change
$249 - Throttle body cleaning
$124 - Brake fluid flush
$119 - Steering fluid flush

I was a bit wary about the prices and so I called up 4-5 other independent garages who had good Yelp reviews and basically got these prices:

- Power steering fluid flushes are not sold by independent garages, but will do them if the customer insists for about $50-$70. So again $119 is pretty steep and sketchy that the Tustin Toyota recommended it as an important item to service.

- Brake fluid flushes are about $40-$70, not $124. Other independent garages again said that this is not a necessary item either.

- Throttle body cleaning are about $72-$140. $249 is a big 77% markup by Tustin Toyota.

- Front brakes change are about $236 from independent garages.

- Timing belt change are about $550-$800.

I decided to go ahead with the Timing belt change and Front brake change since the prices weren't too bad at the dealership so I called in to do so.

I inquired about changing the Water pump too since the labor involved is the same while changing a Timing belt. (If the Water pump isn't replaced and dies at an earlier time than the Timing belt, I'll have to pay for the same labor costs again.)

My service rep said he'd call me back about the Water pump replacement cost and to get approval for other part replacements while the mechanics are at that part of the servicing.

I get no call for the rest of the day. I call in at 7am the next day to check in. No answer, and so I leave a couple of messages. I get a call back from another service rep at about 8:30am letting me know that my first service rep is off for the day and that my truck is done.

I explained that I was supposed to get a call to make sure that I would be able to get other parts replaced while the Timing belt was being replaced, and that I wanted the Water pump replaced as well. The service rep says: "I don't really believe you. You can wait until tomorrow to speak with the original service rep because I don't  know what you agreed on with my colleague - and ... I don't want to talk to the director about this either because he's busy. You can pick up your truck today because the work is done, or you can leave it for the day and talk to my colleague. Thank you."
Not very helpful that my first service rep didn't even tell me he wouldn't be in the office or transfer my case to another service rep properly.

Thats 2 days with my truck in the shop.

My recommendation, check out independent garages. You'll most likely get overcharged at Tustin Toyota, and the customer service needs some major work.</Review>

<Time>1592509238929</Time><Rate>5<//Rate><Review>After retirement, I started to work on house repairs especially the rain gutters that I was constantly cleaning due to trees and that occasionally overflowed.  Of all the companies I contacted, only Byer's returned my note. I already new Byer's was the most expensive in the area, but decided to at least listen.  The initial appointment took almost two hours which will be a turnoff to most, but it was thorough.  One would be hard pressed to find someone willing to buy quality over price.  But it is the most important attribute of any purchase.   And that it what Byer's is offering: a quality product with guarantees that one should expect will be costly.

The technician arrived close to the stated time.  I thought there would be at least two people since my job required adding almost forty feet of extra gutters on the back of the house.   But Jason worked alone out of an enormous truck.  It took almost five hours, but almost everything was premade.  I only supplied a little white paint for the wood where the old gutters had been.

The technician also installed new flashing around the whole house that goes under the tile sheeting.  In short, every possible contingency was anticipated and repaired or replaced by Byer's.

Thank you So Much Byers for a great experience and Thank you Daniel for Outstanding Service.

Thank you Byers!
We had three 160 ISn Solatube Started Kits professionally installed by Byers solar/Roofing in Grass Valley ca.

This is our new House in Yuba City and we have not moved into the house yet but so far, we love them.  They put out just the right amount of light for the rooms we put them in. (2 bathrooms and the laundry room all without windows).
The best way I can compare the amount of light they put out is this:  During a sunny day without clouds the rooms all had the same amount of light as if there were a window in the room and the sun was not shining directly into the window.  Hope that makes sense to you.  What I am trying to say is we are Very happy with the amount of Light in the rooms.

As Far as the Installation went.  in my experience, it is Very Rare these days to have a contractor show up when they say they will, even to give you a quote (or even call to tell you they will be late),  but Daniel, from Byers, was on site on time and ready to go at our appointment time.
He was professional, Polite, and efficient and I felt he completely understood our needs and concerns.  Because this is a new construction there were several obstacles and timing issues we had to overcome, and Byers worked with us.
The biggest issue was that at the time of the first visit Daniel could not complete the installation because the roofing was not complete.  He did install the Roof collectors but could not finish the flashing until the roof was finished which meant he would have to come back.
Normally Byers would change for the return visit to complete this but because of our circumstances they did not charge us extra for that visit.
For the Return visit Daniel was running late due to an unforeseen vehicle issue and he called me  20 minutes before the appointment time to let me know.  Which is Outstanding in my book normally I must call the contractor to see where they are if they are late.
Thank you So Much Byers for a great experience and Thank you Daniel for Outstanding Service.< /Text>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Dr. Robert Puff's podcast on Happiness really resonated with me. He makes you think about one of the harsh realities of life that we face in everyday living - criticism and how it impacts us from truly being happy in life. Criticism in our lives is unavoidable. At some point and in some way we will be criticized.  After all, we cannot please everyone. He talks about the nine steps that we can take to handle criticism in order to find happiness in our personal lives. One of the steps, judging others that he talks about, has to be one of the biggest and most difficult changes that we could all make. After listening to the nine steps, I came away understanding my reactions to criticism and how criticism has over the years impacted me in being happy in my life. I am more knowledgeable, self-aware, confident and ready for the challenges that I will face in life and better equipped to handle criticisms.< /Review>

<response>None</response>< review>
I've been listening to Dr. Puff's podcasts for the last few days, where he explores issues related to happiness: what it means to be happy and how to achieve contentment in life. The setup of his podcasts is simple (him speaking over what sounds like a faint excerpt of Bach's The Well-Tempered Clavier) but the format works amazingly well. The simplicity of the format means less distraction from the weighty themes he's wrestling with, such as the nature of happiness and how dreams relate to it. These are really soothing to listen to before bedtime and they've already given me food for thought about how to evaluate my life. Highly recommended for anyone out there who's reflective and wants five minutes of enrichment to start the day.</review>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I listened to the 58 Happiness - Treating Life as a Permanent Vacation and I must say I really enjoyed it. I'm not too fond of podcasts, but Dr. Puff's podcast helped me realize a few things about how I view my life.

He talked about letting go of things - When we are attached to things, we get upset because we don't want to lose those things when things change. However, if we were to let go, we wouldn't get upset over the things that are not permanent.

Recently, I had a job interview that I have been wanting for the past 4 years. I finally got the interview, but I ended up stuttering and saying the wrong things. I got upset over this because I knew I did horrible. Now I realize that I need to let go of this interview and not be so attached because if not I will not be happy.

This podcast really helped me see things a little bit differently and now I definitely feel like I can be much happier.</review>
